I sorted out my experience of staying this time in detail, and gave some references to families who want to bring their children to Luoyang.
I took my children to travel from Xi'an to Luoyang. Before coming here, I also referred to some information and made corresponding strategies. The price of Huayang Plaza International Hotel is at a high-end level in Luoyang. The room we stayed in cost more than 800 a day. Compared with other economical hotels in Luoyang, in Luoyang There is no advantage in price. But if you count their services, it's a great deal.
First of all, there is a free pick-up station service. Before checking in, call the front desk and explain the time when you arrive at the high-speed rail station. After we get out of the high-speed rail station, the hotel specially sent staff to pick us up with a name card, and then took us all the way to PARKING LOT. They also gave us two hot towels before getting on the bus, because the weather in Luoyang was very hot at that time, we quickly wiped our hands and faces, and then gave us water and boxes of cut fruits, very delicate .
Next, let's talk about the feeling of entering the hotel. A**ospheric, bright, and clean, every staff member will greet each other warmly when they meet each other. Even when going through the formalities, there are special staff members serving tea and handing out snacks to the children. After it was done, someone sent us to the room, and the air machine and air conditioner had been turned on in advance.
After returning to the room, I found that there was a QR code for free services on the table. Because I had a child, I tried to scan the service for free fruit and snacks. I ordered a lot at the time, just to see if it would work It will be delivered, but after a minute, the staff brought a lot of food and several kinds of drinks. Fruit and snacks, this service also continues the next day.
We were also able to use their gym for free during our stay at the hotel. There are also a lot of fitness equipment, and the inside is also very comfortable. The card is placed in the room, just take it and use it.
The room I stayed in was very large, with a bed, a sofa, and a small storage room. I especially liked the hair dryer in their bathroom, which was super easy to use.
If you don't want to go out, you can also order food directly in the hotel room, just scan the code, and it will be delivered in a while.
Then there will be two free breakfasts per room. There are many types of breakfast, clean and tidy, exquisite and delicious. Next to each group of tables, there will be a staff member who keeps collecting the dishes and things on the table, so that you feel tidy at all times.
The hotel room also provides free laundry service every day, you can wash two pieces, put them in the morning, and deliver them in the afternoon.
Generally speaking, the staff of this hotel are also very cohesive. Everyone seems to regard this hotel as their home and love it very much, so they work hard and sincerely.
During the few days we lived, we really had a good experience. Luoyang is a clean and tidy city with low prices. Opposite the hotel is Wanda Plaza and Changshen International Plaza. Dining is convenient and not very expensive. If we come again next time, I will still choose to stay in this hotel, because the various services are of great value Yes, it is definitely the best choice for families with children.

The hotel also arranges 2 pieces/day of free laundry for each room free of charge, as well as free car wash service.

I saw that the staff also prepared a lot of packed lunch boxes, which are probably also packed for the guests staying in the hotel. Next to the restaurant there is also a play area for younger children.

There are 2 shopping malls opposite the hotel for shopping or dining. There is also a 24-hour convenience store for emergency purchases.

Then, there are 2 suggestions for the hotel:
1. The water output of the shower in the bathroom is too small, and it will be much better to replace it with a supercharged one.
2. The floor prompts of the elevator are not clearly visible at all, even if they are pasted with self-adhesive paper, it will be much better.

Really recommend staying at this hotel, the service is very satisfactory.
